<Text>I'd read online that this placed served a Cubano Sandwich, a real favorite when I lived in New York City.  The restaurant is a food counter within a mini food court called The Cookhouse in a very cute retail development called Vail Headquarters.  It's the site of an historic old ranch, with modern theming to match, surrounded by strip malls along Temecula Parkway.  To cut to the chase, I didn't like my Cubano.  The food was high quality, if very pricey and small but certainly large enough to satisfy.  But they used heavily smoked and BBQ-rubbed pork which didn't marry well, I thought, with the traditional Cubano ingredients of swiss cheese, mustard and pickles.  I don't mind "re-inventing" classic foods as long as the result is tasty.  This was just bizarre and kind of unpleasant.  Sorry.  No seating indoors now for Covid 19 but plenty of picnic tables outdoors.  And plenty of free parking adjacent.< /Text><Gmap_id>0x80d954e91ad21717:0xdd965868faa35ec6<//Gmap_id>< rating>

<UserId.>118119001893192250622<//UserId.><username>Sidney Kuo< /username>< Time>
1525224579632< /Time>
< rating>
5<//rating>
< text>
This inconspicuous place is one of my absolute favorite BBQ in San Diego.  Having lived in North Carolina for four years, I have very high standards when it comes to BBQ, especially when it comes to pork.

While a few other BBQ joints have standout briskets such as Grand Ole BBQ or Coop's, none of those places come close to touching The Smok'd Hog's pulled pork.  The pulled pork here is smoked to perfection, lightly smoke kissed and tender without the slightly stinky smell that pork can sometimes have.  This type of pulled pork is exactly what you might have in North Carolina--it's perfect in a sandwich, and also perfect on its own in a plate.

They also have a great selection of BBQ sauces to go with their meats and on the pulled pork sandwich.  I can't speak to the authenticity of the NC sauce, but even in NC itself, there is a variety of different sauces as well, and to be honest the most famous east Carolina sauce is probably way too much vinegar for anyone who is not a native from there.  The other sauces here are good, and with the large selection I'm sure there's one to fit each person's tastes.

In addition to the pork, the pulled chicken is very good as well.  It's smokey and not too dry.  It's also pulled, which distinguishes it from the BBQ chicken at some other places.  After having it in the sandwich with the Alabama white sauce, I had to order an extra half pound of it to go to eat it at home later!

The Cubano here is also quite delicious and has great flavors.  The collard greens have a good meat flavor with a touch of bitterness for balance, and the mac and cheese here has a cheesy texture and good taste without being overly heavy or salty.

Overall, if I lived closer to this place, I'd probably eat it every week.  If you like pulled pork, there is no place in San Diego better than here!<//text>

< name>
Ookla Mok<//name>
<Time>1544639223479< /Time><rating>5<//rating>< Review>
A triumph in smoked meats.  If you're visiting San Diego, you'll probably go to the zoo or Balboa Park.  This puts you in close proximity to some of the best smoked meats & sandwiches around.  Located just beyond the north entry to the park is a small red building on a corner with a smoker out front.  You'll drive past it if you're not looking....and that'd be a huge mistake.  While the lot is very small, find a place to park & step inside the screen door.  What meets your eye isn't pretty but the smells that fill your nose more than make up for it.  In a 5 day visit, I ate at the Smok'd Hog twice (& would have been a 3rd if not for bad traffic our last day).  The first visit, I ordered a pulled pork sandwich with a sweet-heat sauce.  Pulled pork is fairly easy but often underwhelms...but not at the Smok'd Hog.  It was undoubtedly the best I've had.  My wife stole a piece & was hooked.  She wanted one for herself, which setup a return visit a couple of days later.  In that visit, I had a rib meat sandwich, which was also a treat.  The prices are very reasonable & the staff is terrific.  My calendar has been reset from Gregorian to "how many days ago I ate at The Smok'd Hog."  It's been 10 days, by the way, the longest 10 days of my life.
They're 1,000 miles away from my home city & I fear they've ruined smoked meats for me forever.  Was it worth it?  You're damn right is was!< /Review>

I only visited this eatery because of the Yelp and the readers review.. They may have been paid for the star ratings because I did not find it as being a 3.5 or a 4. starred rating out of 5 stars as listed.
My friend and I both had the Plate special.  Pulled Pork , Cornbread + 1 side $16.00. drinks extra. The total dollar spent $39.00 plus $6.00 tip $45.00.   I would have enjoyed Jack in the Box more..
The table tops were sticky, the paper plates, with plastic Knife, fork, and drinking glass. The napkins was the superior choice here at least.
The Pulled Pork , sides and cornbread were served in cardboard containers each. (my Mac and cheese side was extremely dry and the cheese was so overcooked. My friends chose the Cole Slaw, the cabbage was nice however the dressing not so good. (I always that that Best food mayonnaise had some flavor) so they may have chosen a lessor quality. Both of our pulled pork selection had enough oil (grease would be a better chose of words)floated in the cardboard container.
When served at the sticky table, the server/cashier pointed out the different types of BBQ sauces displayed on the table, The containers looked  as thought they had not been cleaned for months,  the actual opening of the containers displayed a half inch of dried contents. Very nasty.  I can not say that the beverages complimented the meal. at least the names enticed the idea of have one.
I would bet the neither of the two people had a required Food Handlers care, or attended a required food preparation and safety class, in person or on line!
Now on the other hand, As being a retired Restaurant owner of two, I can see this place could have a lot of potential hot spot for it's neighborhood location.. I would concentrate on Carry Out for now with Dine In when their act is together including cleaning the serving area and sauce containers.</review>

< text>
Too expensive for secondhand clothing. Come on. A new shirt is literally $15 or more like if it's Michael Kors. But you will find some good clothing. Beat up, faded, torn shoes are literally $30. And people will still buy it and get ripped off. You can probably find identical items for a better condition, cheaper price at another department store like kohl's, Walmart, Sears, etc.
Some Workers are always talking instead of working and helping customers when they're supposed to.
TERRIBLE Management. Horrible, unprofessional, rude manager and supervisors maybe with the exception of 2. Corporate doesn't care if you get bad customer service.
Also, every time  I come, there are always new workers which should tell you something. At the front register, the glass is so scratched you can barely see the jewelry they have there. Messy store too. Store always smells because homeless people come in smelling like body odor
Store needs new look.
And that's my two cents.</text>

< Review>
Ordered here by accident we actually meant to get Yan's China Bistro in Walnut Creek. We were hopeful though, because we live near here now, but we will definitely not be going here again.

The pork chow mein was tasteless and overly greasy, the kung pao chicken was inedible (the pieces of chicken were full of gristle and tasted off). The salt and pepper calamari was okay; I'd eat it.
My spouse was unwell the next morning also. I didn't eat much so I was okay.</Review>

Me and the two roommates ordered via grubhub from here.  They've lived here 8+ years and me about 1.5 years.  1st time experience.  Everything was really good expect the "Scallop with Hot Spicy Garlic Sauce
$14.75 Hot and spicy dish".  There was nothing "hot and spicy" about the dish.  Indeed the 2 rommies, neither of whom can handle spice, tasted it and confirmed that it was sweet and there was nothing spicy about it.

No big deal.  I've worked in food virtually all my life.  Mistakes happen.

Imagine my surprise when I called the restaurant and I was told, after some hemming and hawing, that their "hot spicy" garlic sauce was very sweet.  Furthermore there was nothing that could be done.

Well, yes there could have been more done on the restaurant's part like, truth in advertising,  an offer to remake the dish...........I don't know, maybe just a simple apology.

They came SO close to having 3 regular customers tonight.

It was blown over something that could have easily been remedied.....if they had just tried.<//review>

I went in to purchase a new phone for my mother and in my mind I knew how much I was going to spend because I did my research. I went in and Mark immediately asked me how he may assist me. He was able to give me the BEST deal there was and explained everything throughly. He has a lot of energy and I asked him to repeat several things over and he gladly did. He did not make me feel bad for asking questions and re-explained EVERYTHING just to make sure. Everyone there was really nice and welcoming, including Bobby, David, and Brandon. This has been a great experience and I no longer have to drive 2-3 miles to another T-Mobile store.< /Review>

116384817791981580097< /UserId.>
< Name>
jugglinglessons< /Name>
<Date>1596900218208<//Date>< rating>
2</rating>
< text>
Comparing with my neighbors, T-Mobile is clearly the best data network for my local area.  Visiting the store to add a data line was a most frustrating experience.  When I asked for another of what I already had I was presented with a menu with no explanations.  it took about 20 minutes to land on a plan that was exactly like I had but $9 cheaper a month.  When I asked about forwarding my calls, we try to work it out for a long time and then I was told I can't forward my calls because my phone is a tablet and not a phone.  It acts like a phone I hold it up to my head and make phone calls.  But apparently because it's a tablet I can't forward my calls?  Silly restrictions like that should not be the customer's problem.  Trying to use the T-Mobile app was utterly impossible.  the people behind the counter couldn't get anything more than meaningless errors like our wires are crossed please try again.  I was there for an hour and they gave me misinformation at least every five minutes.  I'm happy with my data plan and I hope I never have to go in there again.  but of course I have to go in there on a different day to try to get my grandfathered plan updated but only on a specific day of the month they can't do it ahead of time because they can't prorate and switch me to a new plan without throwing away part of a month of my service.
Update: T-Mobile responded to this review asking me to send my contact information to them at LosAngelesSouthStoreFeedback@T-Mobile.com and I sent them a polite email that was rejected by the postmaster because they only accept messages from people in their organization or on their whitelist.  Quite funny irony for a company running a data network.</text>

"Bears, Bikers, and Mayhem" has been the slogan of The Lone Star Saloon for decades (although the mayhem is the sort about which everyone says, "Gee! That was fun!"). <Text>Wonderful grounds to walk around on but there are homeless people sleeping and hanging out all day long here. I come here about four times a year with friends and family and have hosted a couple get together/events here. The homeless people sleep under the trees for the shade in the summer and crowd the benches near some of the sculptures. When it rains they sleep under the shelter where the doors are up at the building. On one occasion when I came here with some out-of-town friends a homeless man was bathing himself at the Rock fountain near the trellis and stairs. <rate>1</rate>< review>
Recently me and my grandmother decided to go back to this IHOP after a few months of not going. They had bad habit of making her breakfast on the cool/cold side by leaving it waiting to be brought. This time was even worse. Except for her tea being hot and her pancakes being warm, her food was already cooled when served with the bacon and eggs.
Even mine  the special cheesecake french toast sausage & eggs combo was off. While the french toast was hot, it barely had the cheesecake on it making me ask if order was correct. They decided not to put much apparently. Then had cold sausage and warm enough hash brown/eggs which needed to be eaten fast to make it passable.
We gave this place many chances in the past and they use to be more efficient at serving the food, now they are not. Just save $ and go to BK or McDonalds nearby for breakfast since the food is actually hot.</review>
